 513:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \brief

 594:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** /*******************************************************************************
 595:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * Function Name: Bootloader_Copier
 596:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** ****************************************************************************//**
 597:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  \internal
 598:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  
 599:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  \brief
 600:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    This option is specific for Launcher-Combination architecture only and to 
 601:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    the case when there is a large communication component like BLE. To save 
 602:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    flash space for the user application, such a large communication component 
 603:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    is present only in the first application (Stack application) and is "shared" 
 604:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    with the second application (the user's application actually) by "Code 
 605:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    sharing feature" (See code sharing and BLE Upgradable Stack example project). 
 606:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 607:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n If this option is enabled and the "need-to-copy" flag is set in the second 
 608:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    application's metadata, Copier performs copying of a previously saved Stack 
 609:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    application image from a "temporary location" to the app#1 flash 
 610:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    space (over the current app#1).
 611:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   
 612:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n Before performing the copying operation the new Stack application image 
 613:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    should be received and stored at the temporary location by the current 
 614:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    Stack application. The "need-to-copy" flag should be set in app#2 metadata 
ARM GAS  C:\Users\Kyle\AppData\Local\Temp\ccM9o7ko.s 			page 13


 615:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    indicating that copying operation is required.
 616:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 617:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n The temporary location is half of the flash space that left after Launcher 
 618:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    and 2 metadata rows. This implies that Stack application should fit in 
 619:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    that half of the flash space. 
 620:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 621:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n The destination for the copy operation is obtained as the first row after 
 622:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    Launcher (from app#1 metadata). 
 623:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 624:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n The source of copy operation is the first row of temporary location that 
 625:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    is calculated by the following formula: 
 626:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n     srcRow = (((CY_FLASH_NUMBER_ROWS - dstRow - metaRows) / 2) + dstRow);
 627:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n     where:
 628:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *          - dstRow - the destination's first row (mentioned above);
 629:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *          - CY_FLASH_NUMBER_ROWS - number of all flash rows; 
 630:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *          - metaRows - 2 metadata rows;   
 631:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 632:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n Copying itself means row-by-row copying of the stored application's image.
 633:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    If it fails to copy some row, there is a defined number of attempts 
 634:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    (Bootloader_MAX_ATTEMPTS) to try again. In case of no success, 
 635:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    a user callback function Launcher_CopierCallback() is called. 
 636:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    If it is not defined, then the device is going to be halted.
 637:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * 
 638:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n After performing the application image copying, in case of success 
 639:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    the app#2 metadata is copied in the stead of app#1 metadata and then
 640:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    app#2 metadata is cleared.
 641:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 642:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \n A "need-to-copy" flag is cleared just after performing the app#1 image
 643:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    copying from the temporary location to avoid another consecutive 
 644:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *    copying operation.
 645:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   
 646:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \endinternal 
 647:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *******************************************************************************/

 786:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** 
 787:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** 
 788:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** /*******************************************************************************
 789:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * Function Name: Bootloader_Start
 790:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** ****************************************************************************//**
 791:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \brief
 792:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  This function is called to execute the following algorithm:
 793:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 794:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * -    Validate the Bootloadable application for the Classic Single-app Bootloader or 
 795:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   both Bootloadable/Combination applications for the Classic Dual-app Bootloader/
 796:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   Launch-only Bootloader (Launcher for short) respectively.
 797:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  
 798:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * -    For the Classic Single-app Bootloader: if the Bootloadable application is valid, 
 799:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   then the flow switches to it after a software reset. Otherwise it stays in 
 800:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   the Bootloader, waiting for a command(s) from the host.
 801:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * 
 802:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * -    For the Classic Dual-app Bootloader: the flow acts according to the switching table 
 803:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  (see in the code below) and enabled/disabled options (for instance, auto-switching).
 804:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   NOTE If the valid Bootloadable application is identified, then the control is passed 
 805:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   to it after a software reset. Otherwise it stays in the Classic Dual-app Bootloader 
 806:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   waiting for a command(s) from the host.
 807:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * 
 808:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * -    For the Launcher: the flow acts according to the switching table (see below) and 
 809:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   enabled/disabled options. NOTE If the valid Combination application is identified, then 
 810:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   the control is passed to it after a software reset. Otherwise it stays in the Launcher 
 811:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   forever.
 812:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * 
 813:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * -    Validate the Bootloader/Launcher application(s) (design-time configurable, Bootloader 
 814:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   application validation option of the component customizer).
 815:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * 
 816:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * -    Run a communication subroutine (design-time configurable, the Wait for command 
 817:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *   option of the component customizer). NOTE This is NOT applicable for the Launcher.
 818:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 819:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * -    Schedule the Bootloadable and reset the device.
 820:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 821:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  \ref page_switching_logic
 822:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 823:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \return
 824:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  This method will never return. It will either load a new application and
 825:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  reset the device or jump directly to the existing application. The CPU is
 826:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  halted, if the validation fails when the "Bootloader application validation" 
 827:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  option is enabled.
 828:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  PSoC 3/PSoC 5: The CPU is halted if flash initialization fails.
 829:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *
 830:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** * \details
 831:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  If the "Bootloader application validation" option is enabled and this method
 832:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  determines that the Bootloader application itself is corrupt, this method
 833:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *  will not return, instead it will simply hang the application.   
 834:.\Generated_Source\PSoC5/Bootloader.c **** *******************************************************************************/
